[CREATURE:ELEPHANTAUR_MIDNIGHT]
	[DESCRIPTION:An enormous and sluggish creature with the upper body of a humanoid and the lower body of a elephant-like animal. Its skin is colored black. This evil creature has buff eyes, a trunk, and tusks. It is a grazer. It is a sapient creature. It can open locked doors. It can see very well in the dark. It roams the tropical lands. It can't jump, and despite its body shape, it also can't climb. It can live up to 246 years. Its parts are worth thrice as much as those of normal creatures. It is associated with darkness, depravity, the night, and rumors.]
